	id = CZE_czech.1

	desc = CZE_czech.1.d
	picture = GFX_court

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.1.a executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_czech.3
	title = CZE_czech.3.t
	desc = CZE_czech.3.d
	picture = GFX_internal_faction_business_purchase

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.3.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.3.o1 executed"
		custom_effect_tooltip = CZE_skoda_increased_production_tooltip

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_i
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_ii
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb2_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iii
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb3_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = CZE_skoda_superb_iv
			}
			add_to_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb4_productivity_raw = 100 }
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.3.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.3.o2 executed"
		add_ideas = CZE_skoda_productivity_improved_idea

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_czech.19
	title = CZE_czech.19.t
	desc = CZE_czech.19.d
	picture = GFX_pol_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.19.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.19.o1 executed"
		CZE = {
			country_event = CZE_czech.20
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		army_experience = 30
		add_command_power = 20
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = CZE_czech_polish_military_cooperation
			cost_reduction = 0.2
			uses = 3
			category = CAT_land_doctrine
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -15 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				add = -35
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.19.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_czech.19.o2 executed"
		CZE = {
			country_event = CZE_czech.21
		}
		add_war_support = -0.08
		add_stability = 0.06

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = CZE
				}
				add = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = mbt_hull
					amount = 10
					producer = USA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 80
					producer = USA
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROM = {
					is_in_faction_with = USA
				}
			}
			ROM = {
				army_experience = 15
				country_event = CZE_czech.23
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = Inf_equipment
					amount = 250
					producer = USA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = mbt_hull
					amount = 10
					producer = USA
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = artillery_equipment
					amount = 80
					producer = USA
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}
		CZE = {
			country_event = CZE_czech.24
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				threat > 0.1
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				threat > 0.2
				add = 20
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_czech.22.o2

		add_command_power = -25
		add_political_power = 50

### TV Crisis ###
country_event = {
	id = CZE_TV_Crisis.01
	title = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.t
	desc = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.d
	picture = GFX_czech_tv

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_TV_Crisis.01.a executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_political_power = 50
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.02 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
				20 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.03 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CZE_TV_Crisis.01.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_TV_Crisis.01.b executed"
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.10 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.10 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.04 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
				70 = {
					country_event = { id = CZE_TV_Crisis.05 days = 25 random_days = 5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = CZE_skoda_export_german1_flag
		}

		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -4 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes
		add_timed_idea = { idea = CZE_skoda_superb_i_bought_idea days = 30 }
		clr_country_flag = CZE_skoda_export_german1_flag

		CZE = {
			subtract_from_variable = { CZE_skoda_superb_cars_stockpile = 1000 }

		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = Strike_fighter1
				amount = -15
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 8 }
		modify_treasury_effect = yes

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
	}

			}
		}

			}

country_event = {
	id = CZE_SLO_event.6
	title = CZE_SLO_event.6.t
	desc = CZE_SLO_event.6.d
	picture = GFX_message_signing

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = CZE_SLO_event.6.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_SLO_event.6.a executed"
		clr_country_flag = CZE_SLO_czechoslovakia_start
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CZE
			}
			SLO = {
				annex_country = {
					target = CZE
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_political_power = 200
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_state_core = 117
				add_state_core = 118
				add_state_core = 1017
				add_state_core = 1018
				clr_country_flag = CZE_SLO_czechoslovakia_start
				set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_SLO_czechoslovakia
				news_event = CZE_SLO_event.7
			}
		}
		else = {
			CZE = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SLO
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				add_political_power = 200
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_state_core = 119
				add_state_core = 120
				clr_country_flag = CZE_SLO_czechoslovakia_start
				set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_SLO_czechoslovakia
				news_event = CZE_SLO_event.7
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				has_idea = regional_power
				add = -20
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				add = -40
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CZE_SLO_event.6.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: CZE_SLO_event.6.b executed"
		if = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CZE
			}
			SLO = {
				country_event = CZE_SLO_event.8
			}
		}
		else = {
			CZE = {
				country_event = CZE_SLO_event.8
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = 0.05

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_idea = regional_power
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				add = 40
			}
		}
	}
}
